. * TABLE 1. Persuasion Rates: Papers on Voter Turnout
. *do "$Persuasion/scripts/table1.do"
. 
. * Effects of Uncensored Media: Revisiting Chen and Yang (2019)
. *   To generate the dataset "ChenYang2019.dta", it is necessary to run CY19_data.do 
. *   after downloading the original dataset from 
. *   the AER webpage at https://www.aeaweb.org/articles?id=10.1257/aer.20171765
. *   and storing them at "$Persuasion/data/ChenYang2019".
. *   As the dataset is already created and stored at "$Persuasion/data/ChenYang2019", 
. *   the do file is commented below.
. *do "$Persuasion/scripts/CY19_data.do"
. *   TABLE 2. Persuasion Rates of Exposure to Uncensored Internet
. *do "$Persuasion/scripts/table2.do"
. 
. * Effects of Political News: Revisting Gerber, Karlan, and Bergan (2009) 
. *   TABLE 3. Summary Statistics of the GKB Data
. *do "$Persuasion/scripts/table3.do"
. *   TABLE 4. Estimates of the Key Parameters
. *do "$Persuasion/scripts/table4.do"
. 
. *       TABLE D1. Persuasion Rates: Fox News Effects
. *do "$Persuasion/scripts/tableD1.do"
. 
. *       FIGURE D1. Estimates of Marginal and Average Persuasion Rates
. do "$Persuasion/scripts/figureD1.do"

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1
. *
. * ACKNOWLEDGMENT
. *       The orginal dataset "NTV_Individual_Data.dta" is from Enikolopov, Petrova, and Zhuravskaya (AER, 2011).
. ************
. 
. use "$Persuasion/data/EnikolopovPetrovaZhuravskaya2011/NTV_Individual_Data.dta", clear

. 
. local basic = "logpop98 wage98_ln"

. local sociodem = "male age educ1 married consump"

. 
. local party_list = "Unity OVR"

. 
. *** create outcome variables based on directional treatment ***
. 
. gen y_vote_Unity = 0

. replace y_vote_Unity = 1 if vote_Unity == 0   
(993 real changes made)

. 
. gen y_vote_OVR = 0

. replace y_vote_OVR = 1 if vote_OVR == 1   
(166 real changes made)

. 
. *** predict the exposure rate, that is, e(X,Z) = P(T=1|X,Z) ***
. *** specification: linear in Z and X ***
. 
. probit  Watches_NTV_1999 tvmaxtveloss5050powerA `sociodem' `basic' [pweight=kishweig]

Iteration 0:   log pseudolikelihood = -809.06705  
Iteration 1:   log pseudolikelihood = -741.86673  
Iteration 2:   log pseudolikelihood =  -741.6003  
Iteration 3:   log pseudolikelihood = -741.60028

. predict phat

(4,658 missing values generated)

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.5)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.5)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.5)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1
. *
. * ACKNOWLEDGMENT
. *       The orginal dataset "NTV_Individual_Data.dta" is from Enikolopov, Petrova, and Zhuravskaya (AER, 2011).

. use "$Persuasion/data/EnikolopovPetrovaZhuravskaya2011/NTV_Individual_Data.dta", clear

. 
. local basic = "logpop98 wage98_ln"

. local sociodem = "male age educ1 married consump"

. local party_list = "Unity OVR"

. 
. gen y_vote_Unity = 0

. replace y_vote_Unity = 1 if vote_Unity == 0

. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         probit y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         probit notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         probit watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         logit y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         logit notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         logit watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. do "/Users/sokbaelee/Dropbox/Persuasion/JPE/Replication Files/scripts/figureD1.do"

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1
. *
. * ACKNOWLEDGMENT
. *       The orginal dataset "NTV_Individual_Data.dta" is from Enikolopov, Petrova, and Zhuravskaya (AER, 2011).
. ************
. 
. use "$Persuasion/data/EnikolopovPetrovaZhuravskaya2011/NTV_Individual_Data.dta", clear

. 
. local basic = "logpop98 wage98_ln"

. local sociodem = "male age educ1 married consump"

. 
. local party_list = "Unity OVR"

. 
. *** create outcome variables based on directional treatment ***
. 
. gen y_vote_Unity = 0

. replace y_vote_Unity = 1 if vote_Unity == 0   
(993 real changes made)

. 
. gen y_vote_OVR = 0

. replace y_vote_OVR = 1 if vote_OVR == 1   
(166 real changes made)

. 
. *** predict the exposure rate, that is, e(X,Z) = P(T=1|X,Z) ***
. *** specification: linear in Z and X ***
. 
. reg  Watches_NTV_1999 tvmaxtveloss5050powerA `sociodem' `basic' [pweight=kishweig]
(sum of wgt is 1,209.50712454319)

                                                F(8, 1176)        =      19.36
                                                Prob > F          =     0.0000
                                                R-squared         =     0.1041

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

  9.

.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)

.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1

. predict phat

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. do "/Users/sokbaelee/Dropbox/Persuasion/JPE/Replication Files/scripts/figureD1.do"

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1
. *
. * ACKNOWLEDGMENT
. *       The orginal dataset "NTV_Individual_Data.dta" is from Enikolopov, Petrova, and Zhuravskaya (AER, 2011).
. ************
. 
. use "$Persuasion/data/EnikolopovPetrovaZhuravskaya2011/NTV_Individual_Data.dta", clear

. local sociodem = "male age educ1 married consump"

. predict phat

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1

. predict phat

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.3(0.1)0.7))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.3(0.1)0.7))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,5,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.3(0.1)0.7))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,5,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1
. *
. * ACKNOWLEDGMENT
. *       The orginal dataset "NTV_Individual_Data.dta" is from Enikolopov, Petrova, and Zhuravskaya (AER, 2011).

.

. local sociodem = "male age educ1 married consump"

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.3(0.1)0.7))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.3(0.1)0.7))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,5,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.3(0.1)0.7))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,5,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///

.

. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         logit y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         logit notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         logit watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))

 19.

. do "/Users/sokbaelee/Dropbox/Persuasion/JPE/Replication Files/scripts/figureD1.do"

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1
. *
. * ACKNOWLEDGMENT
. *       The orginal dataset "NTV_Individual_Data.dta" is from Enikolopov, Petrova, and Zhuravskaya (AER, 2011).
. ************
. 
. use "$Persuasion/data/EnikolopovPetrovaZhuravskaya2011/NTV_Individual_Data.dta", clear

. local sociodem = "male age educ1 married consump"

. predict phat

. replace phat = 0.99 if phat > 0.99
(4,658 real changes made)

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         probit y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         probit notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         probit watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. do "/Users/sokbaelee/Dropbox/Persuasion/JPE/Replication Files/scripts/figureD1.do"

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1
. *
. * ACKNOWLEDGMENT
. *       The orginal dataset "NTV_Individual_Data.dta" is from Enikolopov, Petrova, and Zhuravskaya (AER, 2011).
. ************
. 
. use "$Persuasion/data/EnikolopovPetrovaZhuravskaya2011/NTV_Individual_Data.dta", clear

. 
. local basic = "logpop98 wage98_ln"

. local sociodem = "male age educ1 married consump"

. 
. local party_list = "Unity OVR"

. 
. *** create outcome variables based on directional treatment ***
. 
. gen y_vote_Unity = 0

. predict phat

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. do "/Users/sokbaelee/Dropbox/Persuasion/JPE/Replication Files/scripts/figureD1.do"

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1
. *
. * ACKNOWLEDGMENT
. *       The orginal dataset "NTV_Individual_Data.dta" is from Enikolopov, Petrova, and Zhuravskaya (AER, 2011).
. ************
. 
. use "$Persuasion/data/EnikolopovPetrovaZhuravskaya2011/NTV_Individual_Data.dta", clear

. 
. local basic = "logpop98 wage98_ln"

. local sociodem = "male age educ1 married consump"

. 
. local party_list = "Unity OVR"

. 
. *** create outcome variables based on directional treatment ***
. 
. gen y_vote_Unity = 0

. replace y_vote_Unity = 1 if vote_Unity == 0

. *** predict the exposure rate, that is, e(X,Z) = P(T=1|X,Z) ***
. *** specification: linear in Z and X ***
.

>     c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA#c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA ///

. predict phat
(option xb assumed; fitted values)
(4,658 missing values generated)

. *replace phat = 0.01 if phat < 0.01
. *replace phat = 0.99 if phat > 0.99
. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. do "/Users/sokbaelee/Dropbox/Persuasion/JPE/Replication Files/scripts/figureD1.do"

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1
. *
. * ACKNOWLEDGMENT
. *       The orginal dataset "NTV_Individual_Data.dta" is from Enikolopov, Petrova, and Zhuravskaya (AER, 2011).

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. do "/Users/sokbaelee/Dropbox/Persuasion/JPE/Replication Files/scripts/figureD1.do"

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1
. *
. * ACKNOWLEDGMENT
. *       The orginal dataset "NTV_Individual_Data.dta" is from Enikolopov, Petrova, and Zhuravskaya (AER, 2011).
. ************
. 
. use "$Persuasion/data/EnikolopovPetrovaZhuravskaya2011/NTV_Individual_Data.dta", clear

. local sociodem = "male age educ1 married consump"

. 
. *** create outcome variables based on directional treatment ***
. 
. gen y_vote_Unity = 0

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte

 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)

. }

  6.

>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///

.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))

. *** predict the exposure rate, that is, e(X,Z) = P(T=1|X,Z) ***

  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.1(0.4)0.9))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.1(0.4)0.9))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.1(0.4)0.9))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte

 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19.

. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.3(0.2)0.7))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.3(0.2)0.7))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.3(0.2)0.7))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. do "/Users/sokbaelee/Dropbox/Persuasion/JPE/Replication Files/scripts/figureD1.do"

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1
. *
. * ACKNOWLEDGMENT
. *       The orginal dataset "NTV_Individual_Data.dta" is from Enikolopov, Petrova, and Zhuravskaya (AER, 2011).
. ************

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. do "/Users/sokbaelee/Dropbox/Persuasion/JPE/Replication Files/scripts/figureD1.do"

. ************
. * SCRIPT:   figureD1.do
. * PURPOSE:  Creates Figure D1
. *
. * ACKNOWLEDGMENT
. *       The orginal dataset "NTV_Individual_Data.dta" is from Enikolopov, Petrova, and Zhuravskaya (AER, 2011).
. ************
. 
. use "$Persuasion/data/EnikolopovPetrovaZhuravskaya2011/NTV_Individual_Data.dta", clear

. 
. local basic = "logpop98 wage98_ln"

. local sociodem = "male age educ1 married consump"

. 
. local party_list = "Unity OVR"

. 
. *** create outcome variables based on directional treatment ***
. 
. gen y_vote_Unity = 0

. replace y_vote_Unity = 1 if vote_Unity == 0   
(993 real changes made)

. 
. gen y_vote_OVR = 0

. replace y_vote_OVR = 1 if vote_OVR == 1   
(166 real changes made)

. 
. *** predict the exposure rate, that is, e(X,Z) = P(T=1|X,Z) ***
. *** specification: linear in Z and X ***
. 
. qui qui reg Watches_NTV_1999 `sociodem' `basic' ///
>     c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA#c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA /// 
>     c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA#c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA#c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA /// 
>         c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA#i.male c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA#c.age ///
>         c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA#i.educ1 c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA#i.married ///
>         c.tvmaxtveloss5050powerA#c.consump ///
>         [pweight=kishweig]

. predict phat
(option xb assumed; fitted values)
(4,658 missing values generated)

. replace phat = 0.001 if phat < 0.001
(0 real changes made)

. replace phat = 0.999 if phat > 0.999
(4,668 real changes made)

. 
. ***
. 
. foreach party in `party_list' {
  2. 
.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         qui qui reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         qui qui reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         qui qui reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }
(313 real changes made)
(613 real changes made)

Average marginal effects                                 Number of obs = 1,300
Model VCE: Robust

Expression: Linear prediction, predict()
dy/dx wrt:  phat
1._at: phat = .4

.         * generate Y*(1-T)
.     gen notwatch_vote_`party' = 0
  3.         replace notwatch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==0
  4.         
.         * generate Y*T
.     gen watch_vote_`party' = 0
  5.         replace watch_vote_`party' = 1 if y_vote_`party' == 1 & Watches_NTV_1999==1
  6.         
.         * linear probability model of Y given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg y_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
  7.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
  8.         matrix num = r(b)
  9. 
.         * linear probability model of Y*(1-T) given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg notwatch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 10.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 11.         matrix den = J(1,3,1) + r(b)
 12.         
.         * linear probability model of Y*T given X and e(X,Z)
.         * specification: linear in X and quadratic in e(X,Z), while interacting some of X and e(X,Z)
.         reg watch_vote_`party' `sociodem' `basic' ///
>                         c.phat c.phat#c.phat c.phat#c.phat#c.phat  ///
>                         c.phat#i.male c.phat#c.age c.phat#i.educ1 c.phat#i.married c.phat#c.consump ///
>                         [pweight=kishweig]
 13.         
.         margins [pweight=kishweig], dydx(phat) at(phat = (0.4(0.1)0.6))
 14.         matrix num_alt = r(b) + den - J(1,3,1)
 15.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte", st_matrix("num") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 16.         matrix list mte
 17.         
.         mata: st_matrix("mte_alt", st_matrix("num_alt") :/ st_matrix("den"))
 18.         matrix list mte_alt
 19. 
.         matrix results_`party' = (mte \ mte_alt)
 20.         
. }

. do "/Users/sokbaelee/Dropbox/Persuasion/JPE/Replication Files/run.do"

. **********************
. * OVERVIEW
. *   This script generates selected tables for the paper:
. *       "IDENTIFYING THE EFFECT OF PERSUASION" (Sung Jae Jun and Sokbae Lee)
. *   All data are stored in /data
. *   All tables are outputted to /results
. * 
. * SOFTWARE REQUIREMENTS
. *   Stata version 17 or newer
. *
. * PACKAGE REQUIREMENTS
. *   persuasio (can be installed by ssc install persuasio, replace)
. *   outreg (can be installed by ssc install outreg, replace)
. *
. * TO PERFORM A CLEAN RUN, DELETE THE FOLLOWING FOLDER:
. *   $Persuasion/results
. *
. * ACKNOWLEDGMENT
. *       The structure of the replication files is forked from 
. *   Illinois Workplace Wellness Study: Public Use Data Repository
. *   at https://github.com/reifjulian/illinois-wellness-data
. **********************
. 
. **********************
. * Parameters defined by user
. **********************
. 
. * "Persuasion" points to the root directory, which contains the subfolders "data" and "scripts"
. global Persuasion "/Users/sokbaelee/Dropbox/Persuasion/JPE/Replication Files"

. 
. * Number of bootstraps for Table 2
. * The published paper used nbt = 10000. Runtime is approximately 3 hours on an iMac (M1, 2021).
. * Use nbt = 10 to check whether replication code runs without an error. 
. global nbt = 10000

. 
. * set seed for replicability 
. set seed 987975 

. 
. **********************
. **********************
. 
. * Confirm that the global for the root directory has been defined
. assert !missing("$Persuasion")

. 
. * Initialize log and record system parameters
. clear 

. set more off

. cap mkdir "$Persuasion/scripts/logs"

. cap log close
